<h3 id="added" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#added"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Added</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Field</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field.Item</code> component and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">target</code> prop on <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field.Root</code> for multi-control fields (e.g., currency
select + amount input). Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field.Item</code> with a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> to scope controls, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">target</code> to specify which item the
label should focus when clicked.</li>
</ul>

</li>

and other calendar systems)</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { PersianCalendar } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;@internationalized/date&#x27;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">    default</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">      throw</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> new</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> Error</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">`Unsupported calendar: ${</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">identifier</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">}`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">&lt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">DatePicker.Root locale</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;fa-IR&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> createCalendar</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">{createCalendar}</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">&gt;</span></span>

<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Date Picker</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-type</code> attribute to weekend table header and cell</p>

<h3 id="fixed-2" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-2"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Combobox</strong>: Fixed <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> returning empty <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">items</code> array when using controlled value</li>

store</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Radio Group, Listbox, Progress, Segment Group</strong>: Fixed group labels rendering orphan label elements; now render as
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">span</code> per W3C ARIA pattern</li>

<h3 id="fixed-4" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-4"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Auto Resize</strong>: Fixed change event not emitted after clearing controlled textarea</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Date Picker</strong>: Fixed <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">visibleRangeText</code> to show correct format based on current view (year/month/day)</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Dismissable</strong>: Fixed issue where closing a nested dialog/popover would incorrectly close its parent layers</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Menu</strong>: Fixed glitchy submenu behavior when hovering between trigger items quickly</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Checkbox</strong>: Fixed individual checkbox props being overridden by <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">CheckboxGroup</code></li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Collection, Tree View</strong>: Fixed initial focus when first node/branch is disabled</li>

implementing <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">null</code>/<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">undefined</code> checks for date property access.</p>

scrollable container contexts.</p>

<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Angle Slider</strong>: Fix accessibility violation where the slider thumb element lacked an accessible name. The thumb now
supports <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">aria-label</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">aria-labelledby</code> props, and automatically falls back to the label element&#x27;s ID for proper
ARIA labeling.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Select</strong>: Fix accessibility violation where the required state was not set correctly to on the trigger.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Tags Input</strong>: Fix issue where entering a custom tag with combobox integration required pressing <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Enter</code> twice. The
tags-input now correctly handles custom values when the combobox has no highlighted item (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">aria-activedescendant</code> is
empty), allowing the tag to be added on the first <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Enter</code> press.</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="fixed-12" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-12"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>

<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">

<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fix issue where setting initial checked state to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">indeterminate</code> doesn&#x27;t work</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Ensure <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">api.checkedState</code> returns the correct checked state (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">boolean | &quot;indeterminate&quot;</code>)</li>

</li>

<h3 id="added-9" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#added-9"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Added</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Collapsible</strong>: Add support for <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">collapsedHeight</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">collapsedWidth</code> props to control the dimensions of the
collapsible content when in its collapsed state.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Focus Trap</strong>: Allow elements referenced by <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">aria-controls</code> to be included in the trap scope. This makes it possible
for menus, popovers, etc. to be portalled and work correctly.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Pagination</strong>: Add <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">getPageUrl</code> prop for generating <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">href</code> attributes when using pagination as links.</p>
</li>
</ul>

</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="5251---2025-09-27" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#5251---2025-09-27"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>[5.25.1] - 2025-09-27</h2>
<h3 id="fixed-14" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-14"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Date Picker</strong></p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fix issue where year range picker doesn&#x27;t show the hovered range</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fix issue where quarter presets returns incorrect date</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">FormatByte</strong>: Add support for <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">unitSystem</code> property to allow changing between decimal (1000 bytes) and binary (1024
bytes) systems.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Number Input</strong>: When <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">formatOptions</code> is used (like <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">style: &quot;currency&quot;</code>), the cursor would jump to the end of the
input when typing in the middle. The cursor now maintains its relative position during formatting changes.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Pin Input</strong>: Fix issue where using the keyboard shortcuts <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Cmd+Backspace</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Cmd+Delete</code> to delete text in pin
inputs would insert &quot;undefined&quot; instead of clearing the field.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Scroll Area</strong>: Fix issue where resize tracking was not observing the root element, which caused the scrollbar to not
update when the root element&#x27;s size changed.</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="5240---2025-09-14" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#5240---2025-09-14"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>[5.24.0] - 2025-09-14</h2>
<h3 id="added-11" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#added-11"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Added</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Combobox</strong>: Add <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">alwaysSubmitOnEnter</code> prop to allow bypassing the default two-step behavior (Enter to close
combobox, then Enter to submit form) and instead submit the form immediately on Enter press. This is useful for
single-field autocomplete forms where Enter should submit the form directly.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Dismissable</strong>: Add support for layer types in dismissable layer stack. Layers can now be categorized as <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">dialog</code>,
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">popover</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">menu</code>, or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">listbox</code>. This enables:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-nested</code> attribute on nested layers of the same type</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-has-nested</code> attribute on parent layers with nested children of the same type</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--nested-layer-count</code> CSS variable indicating the number of nested layers of the same type</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="changed-3" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#changed-3"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Changed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Hover Card</strong>: Change default delay values for hover card to improve accessibility.</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">openDelay</code>: from <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">700ms</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">600ms</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Tooltip</strong>: Change default delay values for tooltip to improve accessibility.
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.nngroup.com/articles/timing-exposing-content" class="link">Learn more</a></p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">openDelay</code>: from <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">1000ms</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">400ms</code></li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">closeDelay</code>: from <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">500ms</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">150ms</code></li>

<h3 id="removed" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#removed"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Removed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">TimePicker</strong>: The TimePicker component has been removed from this release. This component was never part of the
public API and was considered experimental. It had significant bugs and usability issues across all frameworks and
locales, making it unsuitable for production use.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Migration</strong>: We recommend building a custom time picker using the Select component for simple use cases, or
implementing a time grid pattern for more complex scenarios.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="fixed-17" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-17"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Editable</strong>: Allow text selection in editable preview when <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">autoResize</code> is enabled</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Previously, when <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">autoResize</code> was set to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code>, the preview element had <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">userSelect: &quot;none&quot;</code> applied, preventing
users from selecting text. This has been fixed by removing the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">userSelect</code> style property.</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">File Upload</strong>: Fix regression where clicking the trigger doesn&#x27;t open the file picker when used within the dropzone</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Menu</strong>:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fix issue where keyboard activation of menu items with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">target=&quot;_blank&quot;</code> would open two tabs</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fix issue where hovering a partially visible item with pointer causes it to scroll into view</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Tabs</strong>: Fix issue where <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ids</code> for <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">item</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">content</code> could not be customized</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Toast</strong>: Allow creating a toast store without any arguments</p>
</li>

collection.</li>

<h2 id="5184---2025-08-14" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#5184---2025-08-14"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>[5.18.4] - 2025-08-14</h2>
<h3 id="fixed-23" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-23"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Listbox</strong>: Add support for navigating grid collections</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Carousel</strong>:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fix an issue where the carousel would not update when <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">slideCount</code> or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">autoplay</code> props change.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fix an issue where <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">loop: false</code> was ignored when using autoplay. Now, the carousel will stop when it gets to the
last slide.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">

selection modes</p>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> selection</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> useListSelection</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">({ collection })</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Check if item is selected</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> isSelected</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> selection.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">isSelected</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;React&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Select/deselect items</span></span>

Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">inHoveredRange</code>,

<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-in-hover-range</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-hover-range-start</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-hover-range-end</code>.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Hover range states are only active when not overlapping with actual selected range, enabling distinct styling for
hover preview vs actual selection in range mode.</p>

comparison operations when different date types (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">CalendarDate</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">CalendarDateTime</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ZonedDateTime</code>) are mixed,
particularly in scenarios involving time components.</li>

<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">ListCollection</strong>:Export <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">UseListCollectionReturn</code> type</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">TreeCollection</strong>: Fix issue where the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">filter</code> method completely deletes the children key from the node when there
are no matching children</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Number Input</strong>: Fix issue where default pattern does not allow negative numbers with decimal point</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">File Upload</strong></p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Export <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">FileError</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">FileMimeType</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">FileRejection</code> types</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fix issue where calling <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">api.setFiles</code> invokes validation with incorrect <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">acceptedFiles</code></li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fix issue where the browser might not be able to infer the mime type of a file due to limitations, drag source or
security restrictions. As a fallback in the file validation logic, we now infer the mime type from the file
extension.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h3 id="fixed-33" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-33"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">

differently from clicking with mouse</p>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Toast</strong>: Fix issue where app crashes when <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">toaster.promise</code> is called without loading option. The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">loading</code> option
is now required. A warning will be logged if it is not provided</p>

<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">

<h3 id="changed-6" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#changed-6"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Changed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Collection</strong>: Improve the APIs around <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">tree.flatten(...)</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">flattenedToTree</code> to ensure the original node
properties are preserved.</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Previously, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">tree.flatten()</code> would return an array of objects with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">label</code> stripping out the original
node properties.</p>
</blockquote>

<h3 id="added-23" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#added-23"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Added</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Tree View</strong>: Added support for lazy loading node children. To use this, you need to provide:<!-- -->
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">loadChildren</code> is a function that is used to load the children of a node.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onLoadChildrenComplete</code> is a callback that is called when the children of a node are loaded. Used to update the
tree collection.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Add <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">childrenCount</code> to the node object to indicate the number of children.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">PasswordInput.Control</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">PasswordInput.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span></code></pre>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Select</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onSelect</code> callback that gets fired when an item is selected via keyboard/mouse.</li>
</ul>

<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://ark-ui.com/docs/components/floating-panel" class="link">documentation</a> for details.</li>

<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">New toasts were queued instead of dropped</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Queued toasts were shown when space became available</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Queue cleared when all toasts were removed</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Combobox</strong>:<!-- -->
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fallbacked to the trigger element as the positioning anchor</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-empty</code> attribute to indicate an empty listbox or content</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="520---2025-03-22" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#520---2025-03-22"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>[5.2.0] - 2025-03-22</h2>
<h3 id="added-33" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#added-33"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Added</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">[NEW] DownloadTrigger</strong>: Added Component for downloading a blob or file, whether retrieved synchronously or
asynchronously.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { DownloadTrigger } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;@ark-ui/react/download-trigger&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">export</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> const</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> DownloadImage</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> () </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  async</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> function</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> fetchImage</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">    const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> response</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> await</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> fetch</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;https://picsum.photos/200/300&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">    return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> response.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">blob</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">DownloadTrigger</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> data</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">fetchImage</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> fileName</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;avatar.jpeg&quot;</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> mimeType</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;image/jpeg&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      Download Image</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">DownloadTrigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="changed-8" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#changed-8"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Changed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">NumberInput</strong>: Set the default step to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">0.01</code> when <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">formatOptions.style</code> was set to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">percent</code>.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">[Breaking] Splitter</strong>: Redesigned splitter machine to support more use cases and improve DX. Check out the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://ark-ui.com/docs/components/splitter" class="link">Splitter</a> documentation for more details.</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="fixed-50" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-50"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Toast</strong>: Fixed issue where setting <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">offsets</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">undefined</code> caused the machine to throw.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Select</strong>: Fixed issue where select <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">valueAsString</code> lost reactivity.</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="510---2025-03-17" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#510---2025-03-17"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>[5.1.0] - 2025-03-17</h2>
<h3 id="added-34" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#added-34"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Added</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Added support for a cleanup function in <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ref</code>.</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="fixed-51" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-51"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Field</strong>: Exported the missing <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useField</code> hook.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">NumberInput</strong>: <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> correctly received <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">valueAsNumber</code>.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Slider</strong>: Thumbs initialized correctly when <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">min</code> was set to a non-zero value.</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="501---2025-03-11" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#501---2025-03-11"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>[5.0.1] - 2025-03-11</h2>
<h3 id="fixed-52" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-52"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Effects now flush synchronously instead of using a microtask.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Checkbox</strong>: <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-invalid</code> is no longer set when <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">invalid</code> is <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">false</code>.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Combobox</strong>: Fixed unexpected cursor movement when editing input.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">PinInput</strong>: OTP SMS autofill now works as expected.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">RatingGroup</strong>: Fixed incorrect focus placement on the label.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">TagsInput</strong>: Improved caret detection to prevent unintended tag removal.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Timer</strong>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Fixed slowdown when switching tabs/windows.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Changed default <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">interval</code> from <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">250</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">1000</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="500---2025-03-06" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#500---2025-03-06"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>[5.0.0] - 2025-03-06</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Ark UI just got a major performance boost! 🚀</p>
<h3 id="whats-new-in-v5" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#whats-new-in-v5"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>What’s new in v5?</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Blazing-fast performance</strong> – Every component runs smoother and renders faster.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Smaller bundle size</strong> – Leaner components and adapters for a more efficient build.</li>
</ul>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">We made this happen by using React’s native reactive primitives instead of external stores.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">In our stress tests with <strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">10,000 components</strong>, Ark v5 delivered <strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">1.5x–4x</strong> better performance across the board.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><img src="/static/v5-14071630.svg" alt="Performance comparison showing Ark v5 is 1.5x-4x faster than other libraries" class="mt_2em mb_2em"/></p>
<h3 id="a-quick-note-on-tests" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#a-quick-note-on-tests"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>A quick note on tests</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Most component updates are non-breaking, but due to this change, some tests may need adjustments. For example:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Before</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">it</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;should open by default&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, () </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  render</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">ComponentUnderTest</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> defaultOpen</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  expect</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(screen.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getByRole</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;dialog&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)).</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">toBeInTheDocument</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">})</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// After</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">it</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;should open by default&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">async</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> () </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  render</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">ComponentUnderTest</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> defaultOpen</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  expect</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">await</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> screen.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">findByRole</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;dialog&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)).</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">toBeInTheDocument</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">})</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="added-35" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#added-35"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Added</h4>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Carousel</strong>: ⚠️ Breaking change: Added required prop <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">slideCount</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Carousel.Root</code> component.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Clipboard</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultValue</code> props.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">ColorPicker</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultFormat</code> prop.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Combobox</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultHighlightedValue</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultInputValue</code> props.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">DatePicker</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultFocusedValue</code> prop, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">getViewProps</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">visibleRangeText</code>.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">HoverCard</strong>: Expanded interaction handlers.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Menu</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultHighlightedValue</code> prop.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Pagination</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultPageSize</code> prop.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">PinInput</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">count</code> prop for better SSR aria-label.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Progress</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">locale</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">formatOptions</code> props.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">QrCode</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">pixelSize</code> prop.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Select</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultHighlightedValue</code> prop.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">TagsInput</strong>: Added <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultInputValue</code> prop.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Toggle</strong>: Reintroduced toggle machine.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="fixed-53" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-53"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed</h4>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Accordion</strong>: Fixed issue in Safari where clicking triggers didn&#x27;t show content.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Avatar</strong>: Fixed <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">api.setSrc</code> not working.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Carousel</strong>: Fixed pagination sync and initial page issues.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">File Upload</strong>: Fixed drag-and-drop when <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">directory: true</code>.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Menu</strong>: Fixed context menu positioning not updating on right-click.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Number Input</strong>: Fixed <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> prop not being consumed.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Pin Input</strong>: Fixed focus warnings and editing issues.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Progress</strong>: Allowed more precise (decimal) values.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Radio Group, Switch</strong>: Improved focus behavior in Safari.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Select</strong>: Fixed regression where <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">multiple: true</code> didn&#x27;t work.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Steps</strong>: Ensured ARIA attributes use valid values and wrapped <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">&lt;li&gt;</code> elements correctly within <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">&lt;ul&gt;</code> or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">&lt;ol&gt;</code>.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Textarea</strong>: Fixed <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ResizeObserver</code> warning.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Timer</strong>: Fixed stopping issue when switching tabs; resolved issue where <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">action</code> prop was passed to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ActionTrigger</code>.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Toast</strong>: Fixed keyboard navigation skipping close button.</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Toggle Group</strong>: Fixed <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-focus</code> not being removed on blur.</li>
